# Split Flow Testing Master README

## Document Purpose and Audit Scope
This document is a long-form, accuracy-first testing chronicle for Split Flow as of **February 23, 2026**. It catalogs all relevant test assets in this repository, documents every executed Jest test case line from the latest validated runs, explains why each test matters, and records the historical failure-to-green path.

### Scope Policy
- Included: Backend unit (`backend/src/**/*.spec.ts`), backend e2e (`backend/test/*e2e-spec.ts`), frontend unit (`Investor_app/src/**/*.test.js`).
- Inventory-included but not executed in this run: Detox native e2e assets, k6/perf smoke scripts, legacy Selenium Python suites.
- Legacy Selenium (`Investor_app/tests/*.py`) is documented as **excluded from native-focused validation**; those suites target Expo Web (`http://localhost:8081`).

## Environment and Execution Context
- Validation date (absolute): `2026-02-23`
- Host context: Windows, local workspace execution.
- Backend test command family: `npm test`, `npm run test:e2e`, `npm run test:cov`.
- Frontend test command family: `npm test`, `npm run test:coverage`.
- Result JSON artifacts used for case-level accuracy:
  - `backend/test-results-unit.json`
  - `backend/test-results-e2e.json`
  - `Investor_app/test-results-unit.json`

## Test Strategy Map
- Backend unit tests: deterministic module/service/controller behavior, DTO/guard/strategy logic, and branch-heavy business rules.
- Backend e2e tests: integrated HTTP + auth + persistence behavior, contract verification, security hardening, and concurrency conditions.
- Frontend unit tests: RN component rendering, hooks, context state, API wrapper/interceptor behavior, and utility-level transformations.
- Security emphasis: authn/authz, token lifecycle, payload validation boundaries, privilege boundaries, brute-force/rate-limit behavior, response-shape safety.
- Performance/load tooling (inventory): k6 and smoke scripts for staged execution against running targets.

## Historical Testing Saga (Failure to Green)
### Chronology
- **February 23, 2026 (earlier cycle)**: `finance.service.spec.ts` showed repeated failures tied to chainable Mongoose mock behavior and constructor semantics for ledger model.
- Failure patterns documented in `Investor_app/recent_chat_progress.md` included:
  - non-chainable query mocks causing `.skip is not a function` during spending search flows;
  - `ledgerModel` not constructable (`this.ledgerModel is not a constructor`);
  - project access mock shape mismatches leading to forbidden/not-found in ledger and summary tests;
  - assertion drift (`totalApproved` expectation vs current `approvedSpent` contract shape).
- **Same date, stabilization cycle**: finance test mock corrections and expectation alignment reduced failures from 8 -> 5 -> 3 -> 0.
- **Security expansion cycle**: added/validated broader security hardening and token/account lifecycle test coverage across backend e2e.
- **Final validated state (February 23, 2026)**: all executed backend unit, backend e2e, and frontend unit suites green.

## Security Testing Coverage
Security-relevant validation is covered across backend unit/e2e and frontend interceptor tests.

### Backend security-focused suites and concerns
- `backend/test/security.e2e-spec.ts`: JWT protection, tampered token rejection, outsider project access denial, invite/spending privilege enforcement, role escalation protection.
- `backend/test/security.hardening.e2e-spec.ts`: whitelist enforcement, NoSQL-injection-shaped input handling, profile tampering defenses, body-size limits (`413`), logout/refresh invalidation path, brute-force throttling behavior.
- `backend/test/security.tokens-account.e2e-spec.ts`: disposable email rejection, token misuse checks, export-data secrecy guard (`passwordHash` absent), delete-account re-auth and post-delete login denial.
- Additional contract and concurrency suites include security-adjacent checks on response shapes and concurrent governance actions.

### Frontend security-focused suites and concerns
- `Investor_app/src/services/__tests__/api.interceptors.test.js`: token attachment, refresh retry logic, concurrent 401 coalescing, token clearing on refresh failure or malformed refresh response.
- `Investor_app/src/services/__tests__/api.stress.test.js`: high-volume normalization and dedup flow stability (defensive client behavior under large payload volumes).

## Performance and Load Testing Coverage
### Included as test assets (not executed in this validation run)
- `backend/scripts/k6-load.js`: load scenario scaffolding for request latency/throughput observations.
- `backend/scripts/k6-security.js`: security-oriented k6 scenario focusing on defensive status behavior under pressure.
- `backend/scripts/perf-smoke.js`: smoke-level performance check harness.
- `backend/scripts/security-smoke.js`: security smoke automation script.

### Why not executed here
- These scripts require live target services, scenario tuning, and environment/runtime dependencies outside the deterministic unit/e2e pass used for this audit document.

## Native vs Legacy Test Track Decisions
- Native RN validation track: Jest unit suites + Detox assets in `Investor_app/e2e`.
- Legacy Web Selenium track: Python suites under `Investor_app/tests` currently targeting Expo Web (`localhost:8081`).
- Current policy used in this document: native-focused release validation excludes Selenium web track from pass/fail gating while still fully documenting its existence.

## Coverage Results and Interpretation
### Backend coverage headline (`npm run test:cov -- --watch=false`)
- Raw line: `All files                        \|   84.25 \|    62.24 \|   80.31 \|   85.96 \|`
- Interpreted: Statements **84.25%**, Branches **62.24%**, Functions **80.31%**, Lines **85.96%**.
- Threshold posture: statements/lines exceed 80%; functions exceed 80%; branches remain lower and are primary expansion target.

#### Backend top hotspot modules (from latest report)
- `backend/src/auth/auth.service.ts`: lower coverage in social auth/edge-token paths.
- `backend/src/finance/finance.service.ts`: large surface area with many branch-heavy and export/analytics edge paths.
- `backend/src/projects/projects.controller.ts`: controller branches and role-path combinations.
- `backend/src/uploads/uploads.controller.ts`: lower branch/function coverage.

### Frontend coverage headline (`npm run test:coverage -- --watch=false`)
- Raw line: `All files                \|   80.12 \|    65.85 \|    76.6 \|   80.35 \|`
- Interpreted: Statements **80.12%**, Branches **65.85%**, Functions **76.60%**, Lines **80.35%**.
- Threshold posture: statements/lines exceed 80%; branch and function depth can be expanded further in stateful workflow modules.

#### Frontend top hotspot modules (from latest report)
- `Investor_app/src/services/api.js`: broad surface and lower function/line coverage relative to core utilities.
- `Investor_app/src/context/AuthContext.js`: auth flow branch complexity.
- `Investor_app/src/hooks/useSpendingLogic.js`: branch-heavy spending interactions.

## Known Warnings, Non-Blocking Findings, and Residual Risk
- Backend expected warning path during oversized payload security check: `PayloadTooLargeError` stack trace appears in logs while test asserts `413` behavior.
- Backend finance debug warning path appears (`[approvals-debug]`) during specific approval mismatch instrumentation tests.
- Frontend `LoginScreen` tests emit React `act(...)` warnings due animated updates in test runtime; suite still passes.
- Jest worker-exit warning occasionally appears (`failed to exit gracefully`), indicating possible timer/resource cleanup noise; no failing assertions in latest validated runs.

## Final Status Snapshot
- Total suites executed and passing: **62**
- Total test cases executed and passing: **764**
- Backend unit: **32 suites, 567 tests, all pass**.
- Backend e2e: **9 suites, 47 tests, all pass**.
- Frontend unit: **21 suites, 150 tests, all pass**.
- Coverage posture:
  - Backend statements/lines above 80%.
  - Frontend statements/lines above 80%.

## Appendix A: Commands Used
```bash
cd backend && npm test -- --watch=false --json --outputFile=test-results-unit.json
cd backend && npm run test:e2e -- --watch=false --json --outputFile=test-results-e2e.json
cd backend && npm run test:cov -- --watch=false
cd backend && npm run test:cov -- --watch=false > test-cov-output.log 2>&1
cd Investor_app && npm test -- --watch=false --json --outputFile=test-results-unit.json
cd Investor_app && npm run test:coverage -- --watch=false
cd Investor_app && npm run test:coverage -- --watch=false > test-coverage-output.log 2>&1
```
